STK170:':':
:6 ne " 170":end:
:8 gt "":end:
:@pw="AA":goto SAA170:
:@pw="AB":goto SAB170:
:@pw="AC":goto SAC170:
:@pw="AD":goto SAD170:
:@pw="AE":goto SAE170:
:@pw="ZZ":goto SZZ170:
::end:

:3="   7601":select:
::end:

:(3="   7605" OR 3="   7606") AND 4 co "ST":select:
::end:
SAC170:::
:3="   7605" OR 3="   7606":select:
::end:
SAD170:::
:(3="   7613" OR 3="   7614") AND 4 co "136":select:
::end:

:3="   7613" OR 3="   7614":select:
::end:

::end:

STK101:':':
::'NEXT TWO LINES - COOPER STOCK PO's RUN ONLY ON MON'S:
:DOW(@td,"1") = "TUE" AND @td = "09/04/18":goto diffDay:
:DOW(@td,"1") = "MON" AND @td = "07/30/18":exit:
